 aam chunaav kii tazaa khabaron se apadet rahane ke liesbscrib karenajatak kaa ellection special newzlator The ruling Samajwadi Party (SP) in Uttar Pradesh split into two on Sunday
 'asanvaidhanik' qaraar die gaye party ke rashtriya adhiveshan main mukhyamantri akhilesh yadav ko adhyaksh banaae jane se naaraaz sapa netaa mulaayam singh yadav ne sammelan main paarit sabhi prastaavon ko avaidh qaraar dete hue aayojan ke kartadharta sapa mahasachiv ramgopal yadav tathaa usamen shaamil party upaadhyaksh kiranmay nanda or mahasachiv naresh agarwal ko party se nikaal diya
 Not only this, Mulayam Singh Yadav, Shivpal Yadav and Amar Singh will meet the Election Commission in Delhi on Monday to demand the party's national session to be declared illegal and complain against the decision taken in it
 sapa mahasachiv ramgopal yadav dwaara bulaae gaye rashtriya adhiveshan main akhilesh kii sapa adhyaksh ke rup main tajposhi kar di gai or mulaayam ko party kaa sangrakshak ghoshit kiya gaya
 At the same time, National General Secretary Amar Singh, who is believed to be the root of the quarrel, was removed from the party, while Shivpal Yadav was removed from the post of SP State President
 adhiveshan main kiranmay nanda, naresh agarwal, revati raman singh or ramgovind choudhary samet sapa ke tamaam varisht netaa, zyaadaatar vidhayak or vidhanparishad sadsy tathaa jilon ke padaadhikari shaamil hue
 This showed that the SP is now virtually broken, with just the formality remaining
 rashtriya adhyaksh banane ke baad akhilesh ne apane pehle aadesh main vidhanparishad sadsy naresh uttam patel ko party kaa pradesh adhyaksh niyukt kiya
 All those senior leaders sitting on the stage raised their hands and supported the proposal to make Akhilesh the national president of the party, who was once a neighbor of Mulayam
 duusare prastaav ke tahat mulaayam singh yadav ko sapa kaa sarvocch sangrakshak banaaya gaya, jabaki tisare prastaav ke tahat shivpal singh yadav ko sapa ke pradesh adhyaksh pad se tatkaal hataaya gaya or party mahasachiv amar singh ko sapa se tatkaal nishkasit kar diya gaya
 However, shortly before the commencement of the session, Mulayam issued a letter warning him of action against the leaders and activists who attended it, terming it as 'unconstitutional'
 mulaayam singh ne aanan-fanan main sapa ke sansadeey board kii baithak bulaai, jisamen adhiveshan ke tamaam faislon ko avaidh qaraar diya gaya
 He also expelled party vice-president Kiranmay Nanda and general secretary Naresh Aggarwal, along with Ram Gopal Yadav, the party's leader
 ramgopal ko shanivaar ko hi party main dobaaraa waapas liya gaya tha
 Aggarwal said that now that Akhilesh is his national president, Mulayam has no right to remove him from the party
 shivpal yadav dwaara 'twit' kiye gaye bina letters head vaale ek patr ke anusaar, sansadeey board kii baithak main sapa pramukh dwaara gat 28 disambar ko jari pratyaashiyon kii suchi ko anumodith karte hue bachi hui siton par ummidavaaron ke chayan ke liye mulaayam ko adhikrut kiya gaya
 According to the letter, the Parliamentary Board has also decided to convene the party's National Conclave on January 5 to clear the "confusion" that has spread after Sunday's session
 baharhaal, aaj ke adhiveshan ke baad akhilesh samarthak jabaran sapa karyaalay main ghus gaye or pradesh adhyaksh ke kaksh ke baahar lagi shivpal yadav kii nem plate ukhadkar phenk di
 Naresh Uttam Patel, the newly appointed state president, also took over his assignment immediately
 rashtriya adhyaksh banaae jane ke baad akhilesh yadav ne kaha ki vah hameshaa mulaayam singh kaa sammaan karte the or ab pehle se zyada sammaan karte hai
 When every section of society had made up its mind to form SP government again, only then some forces got involved in the conspiracies
 ab pradesh main jab dobaaraa sapa kii sarkaar banegi to sabase zyada khushi netaji ko hogi
 Emotionally Akhilesh said that Netaji's position is at the top
 unhen dar tha ki chunaav se ain pehle 'naa jane koun milakar unase (mulaayam) kya kara detaa
 If i have to make any sacrifice for the party, i will '
 unhone kaaryakartaaon ko dhanyavad dete hue aahwan kiya ki aane vaale do-dhai maheene bahut mahatvapurn hai
 a secular government is to be formed in the state, which can take it on the path of prosperity
 iske purv, ramgopal yadav ne apane sambodhan main kaha ki party or sarkaar kaa kaam bahut thik tareeke se chal rahaa tha or usee dauraan party ke do vyaktiyon ne sajeesh karke akhilesh ko pradesh adhyaksh pad se hatwa diya
 a crisis arose again in the party
 unhone kaha ki party main tikaton kaa bantwaaraa manamaane dhang se hone laga tha
 The state president continued to take arbitrary unconstitutional decisions on behalf of the national president
 jo log party ke sadsy bhi nahin he, unhen tikat die gaye
 It was clear that people did not want it at any cost, won the SP elections and Akhilesh again became the Chief Minister
 ramgopal yadav ne kaha ki pani jab sir se upar nikal gaya tab party ke hajaaron kaaryakartaaon ne vishesh adhiveshan bulaane kii likhit maang kii thi
 We waited for two months to improve
 tab yah nirnay liya gaya ki party kaa vishesh apatkaaleen adhiveshan bulaayaa jaae
 It is known that Mulayam Singh Yadav expelled both Ram Gopal and Akhilesh from the party for six years on Friday, regarding Ram Gopal's decision to call the National Representative Conference of SP on January 1
 tippaniyan After the gathering of more than 200 mlas at the meeting of the Legislature Party convened by Akhilesh on Saturday at his residence and the arrival of very few candidates in the meeting of candidates called by Mulayam at the party's state headquarters and after the mediation of senior SP leader, Mulayam The expulsion of Akhilesh and Ram Gopal was canceled
 haalanki donon kii barkhaastagi kii mukhya vajah bane rashtriya adhiveshan ko bulaane kaa faisla barkaraar rakhaa gaya tha
 (this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) yahi nahin mulaayam singh yadav, shivpal yadav or amar singh somvaar ko dilli main chunaav ayog se milakar party ke rashtriya adhiveshan ko avaidh ghoshit karne kii maang karenge or usamen liye gaye faisale ke kilaaf shikaayat karenge
 At the national convention convened by SP General Secretary Ram Gopal Yadav, Akhilesh was crowned as SP president and Mulayam was declared the party's mentor
 vahiin, jhagade kii jad maane ja rahe rashtriya mahasachiv amar singh ko party se nikaal diya gaya, jabaki shivpal yadav ko sapa ke pradesh adhyaksh pad se hataa diya gaya
 The session was attended by all senior leaders of SP including Kiranmay Nanda, Naresh Aggarwal, Revathi Raman Singh and Ramgovind Chaudhary, mostly mlas and mlas and district officials
 isse jaahir ho gaya ki sapa ab vaastavik rup se tut chuki he, bas aupchaarikta bhar baaki he
 After becoming national president, Akhilesh in his first order appointed Legislative Council member Naresh Uttam Patel as the state president of the party
 manch par baithe un tamaam varisht netaaon ne haath uthaakar akhilesh ko party kaa rashtriya adhyaksh banane ke prastaav kaa samarthan kiya, jo kabhi mulaayam ke bagalgir the
 Under the second resolution, Mulayam Singh Yadav was made the highest patron of the SP, while under the third resolution Shivpal Singh Yadav was immediately removed from the post of the state president of the SP and party general secretary Amar Singh was immediately expelled from the SP
 haalanki adhiveshan shuru hone se kuch hi der pehle mulaayam ne ek chitthee jari kar ise 'asanvaidhanik' bataate hue isamen shaamil hone vaale netaaon evam kaaryakartaaon ke khilaaf karrwai kii chetavanee di thi
 Mulayam Singh hurriedly called a meeting of the Parliamentary Board of the SP, in which all the decisions of the session were declared invalid
 saath hi unhone adhiveshan ke kartadharta ramgopal yadav ke saath-saath usamen shirkat karne vaale party upaadhyaksh kiranmay nanda or mahasachiv naresh agarwal ko party se nikaal diya
 Ram Gopal was recalled to the party on Saturday itself
 agarwal ne kaha ki ab akhilesh unke rashtriya adhyaksh hai, lihaaja mulaayam ko unhen dal se nikaalane kaa koi haq nahin he
 According to a letter with no letter head 'tweeted' by Shivpal Yadav, while approving the list of candidates released by the SP chief on December 28 in the parliamentary board meeting, Mulayam was authorized to select the candidates for the remaining seats
 Gone
 khat ke mutabik, sansadeey board ne ravivaar ke adhiveshan ke baad faile 'bhram' ko dur karne ke liye aagaamee paanch janvari ko party kaa aakasmik rashtriya adhiveshan bulaane kaa nirnay bhi liya he
 However, after today's session, Akhilesh supporters forcibly entered the SP office and uprooted Shivpal Yadav's name plate outside the state president's chamber
 'navaniyukt pradesh adhyaksh' naresh uttam patel ne apana kaarybhaar bhi fouran grahan kar liya
 After being made national president, Akhilesh Yadav said that he always respected Mulayam Singh and now respects him more than ever
 jab samaaj kaa har varg sapa kii dobaaraa sarkaar banane kaa man bana chukaa tha, tabhi kuch takatein sajishon main jute gayi
 Now when the SP government is formed again in the state, Netaji will be most happy
 bhavuk hue akhilesh ne kaha ki netaji kaa sthaan sabase upar he
 He was afraid that before the elections, who would not have known him (mulayam)
 mujhe party ke liye koi bhi tyaag karnaa hoga, to main karuunga'
 He thanked the workers and called upon them that the next two-and-a-half months are very important
 pradesh main ek aisi dharmanirpeksh sarkaar banani he, jo use khushhaali kii raah par le ja sake
 Earlier, Ram Gopal Yadav said in his address that the work of the party and the government was going on very well and at the same time, two persons of the party conspired to remove Akhilesh from the post of state president
 party main phir ek sankat paidaa ho gaya
 He said that the distribution of tickets in the party was arbitrary
 pradesh adhyaksh rashtriya adhyaksh kii taraf se manamaane asanvaidhanik faisle lete rahe
 Those who are not even members of the party were given tickets
 spasht tha yah log kisi bhi keemat par nahin chaahate the, sapa chunaav jite or akhilesh phir mukhyamantri bane
 Ramgopal Yadav said that when the water got above the head, thousands of party workers had written a written demand to call a special session
 hamane do maheene tak sudhaar kaa intjaar kiya
 It was then decided that a special emergency session of the party be called

 a post shared by Abhishek Bachchan (@bachchan) on Jun 10, 2017 at 11:02 pm PDT # throwbackthursday taken in the mid 80's (1985 if memory serves)
 i call it Big b and the Bachchan bunch
 Dad was hospitalized with Mysthenia Gravis and my sister, cousins and i had gone to visit him
 Being too young to understand what all was going on our parents always made it out to be like an outing so that we would not be disturbed by the hospital and its workings
 When i used to visit my father after his accident on the sets of "coolie" in 1982, seeing him connected to many drips and machines, he used to tell me they were kites that he had got for me
 i was 6 yrs old
 My father was fighting for his life and all i thought about was
